      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              ES Localization Services was established in 1994 as a software localization company, and is the leading company in its field in Turkey. A fast developing company, ES opened an office in Cairo, Egypt in 2004, and continues to take confident steps towards becoming the most successful localization company for regional languages, especially Turkish and Arabic.

Since it was established, ES has worked with the leading software and hardware companies of the world and produced top quality results that have satisfied its clients. ES has achieved its respected position within the industry both due to directly work-related factors, such as on-time delivery, and its other qualities such as work ethic, integrity and professionalism.

ES, which continually tries to provide the best service possible to its clients by focusing on their requirements and expectations, is a member of professional associations such as ALC, GALA and ATA, which allows us to follow and contribute to changes in the industry and technology.

ES' Quality is certified with EN 15038 AND ISO 17100 for years.
          </p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Absolutely spot on üëèüèª 

As <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/renatob?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Renato Beninatto</a> highlights here, when I stepped into localization industry last year, many voices were asking the same question: ‚ÄúIs localization over? Will AI take it all?‚Äù

The truth is, industries don‚Äôt simply vanish, they transform. What matters is the ability to adapt. 

At <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/company/es-localization-services-ltd?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>ES Localization Services Jsc.</a>, we see technological progress not as a threat, but as an opportunity. <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fai&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#AI</a> and <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fautomation&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#automation</a> empower us to refine processes, work more efficiently, and deliver faster than ever before. At the end of the day, human expertise remains essential. Cultural fluency, creativity, and insight cannot be automated yet.

Our vision is clear: embrace innovation, evolve with it, and ensure that technology and human talent work hand in hand to create lasting impact. üåç‚ú®

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="feed-reshare-content__commentary">When someone tells you ChatGPT is going to kill localization, show them this: 

<a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/dDbPKTrZ?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/dDbPKTrZ</a>

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/openai?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>OpenAI</a>  is currently hiring a Localization Manager to "drive localization strategy and execution across marketing surfaces," partner with product and engineering teams on internationalization infrastructure, and "pilot AI-first translation workflows with human-in-the-loop review."

The role involves managing vendor relationships, linguist sourcing across priority markets, and delivering localized experiences for <a class="link" href="http://openai.com?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>openai.com</a>, <a class="link" href="http://ChatGPT.com?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>ChatGPT.com</a>, campaigns, and educational content.

Sound familiar? We had similar conversations about <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/google?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Google</a>  and <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/microsoft?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Microsoft</a> when their machine translation solutions emerged. Everyone thought that they would revolutionize translation overnight. Today, they're among the world's largest purchasers of localization services.

The pattern repeats itself: the companies building the most sophisticated language technology inevitably become the ones who understand best why human expertise remains indispensable. They know that translating words is just the beginning ‚Äì localizing experiences requires cultural fluency, market understanding, and that irreplaceable human touch. They are not buying words, they are buying results. 

OpenAI hiring a localization team is the validation that you needed.

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Flocalization&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#localization</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Ftranslation&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#translation</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fai&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#AI</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fchatgpt&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#ChatGPT</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fopenai&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#OpenAI</a></p>
